	id = GNG_silicon_dreams_on_the_pearl_river
	icon = GFX_focus_GNG_silicon_dreams_at_pearl_river

	x = 8
	y = 0

	allow_branch = {
		has_country_flag = chief_executive_suzuki
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = yasuda_crisis
		}
	}
	cost = 4.286

	completion_reward = {
		country_event = {
			id = guangdong.1
			hours = 6
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_flavor.5
				days = 25
			}
			country_event = { # Starting Hyperwar chain
				id = guangdong_YakuzaTriadHyperwar.1
				days = 180
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_unlocks_google_maps_gui
		set_country_flag = GNG_Google_Maps_Show
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = GNG_Growing_Kenpeitai_Influence
			activate_mission = GNG_Growing_Yakuza_Influence
			activate_mission = GNG_Growing_Triad_Influence
			activate_mission = GNG_Growing_Police_Influence
		}
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = GNG_subsidize_the_launch
	icon = GFX_focus_GNG_subsidize_launch

	relative_position_id = GNG_identify_the_breakthroughs
	x = 0
	y = 1

		focus = GNG_identify_the_breakthroughs
	}
	cost = 2.143

	completion_reward = {
		add_to_variable = { GNG_product_cycle_tracker = 1 } #Indicates that the 1962 Product Cycle has been done
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.050 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		add_political_power = 30
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GNG_1962_cycle = 0 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_subsidize_the_launch_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GNG_1962_cycle = 1 } }
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong.11
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GNG_1962_cycle = 2 } }
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong.12
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GNG_1962_cycle = 3 } }
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong.13
				hours = 6
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { GNG_1962_cycle = 4 } }
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong.10
				hours = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

	icon = GFX_focus_GNG_plug_the_leak
	x = -1
	y = 1
	cost = 2
	relative_position_id = GNG_no_quarter

	prerequisite = {
		focus = GNG_from_the_ground_up
		focus = GNG_once_again_asking
	}

	prerequisite = {
		focus = GNG_no_quarter
		focus = GNG_an_invisible_cage
	}

	prerequisite = {
		focus = GNG_no_connection_shall_go_unused
		focus = GNG_no_resource_shall_go_untapped
	}

	prerequisite = {
		focus = GNG_our_camaraderie_lasts_forever
		focus = GNG_our_model_reigns_supreme
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GNG_plug_the_leak"
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_plug_the_leak_tt
		country_event = {
			id = guangdong_fujitsuOC.33
			hours = 6
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_fujitsuOC.48
				days = 20
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_gdp_growth = 0.5 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_status_dynmod_rgdp = 1 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_status_product_profitability_modifier = 0.1 }
		add_to_variable = { GNG_status_product_seats_modifier = 0.1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_rgdp_dynmod_recover_oc
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
}

		}

		}
	}

			limit = {

				id = guangdong_fujitsuOC.39
				hours = 6
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_temp_variable = { sar_spt_temp = 3.5 }
				GNG_police_control_change = yes
				set_temp_variable = { zhu_app_temp = 2 }
				GNG_zhujin_app_change = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_our_loyalest_guardians_not_passed
			country_event = {
				id = guangdong_fujitsuOC.40
				hours = 6
			}
			every_owned_state = {

				GNG_police_control_change = yes

			}
		}

			set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Temp = -2 }

shared_focus = {
	id = GNG_our_greatest_assets
	icon = GFX_focus_GNG_our_greatest_assets
	x = 1
	y = 1
	cost = 2
	relative_position_id = GNG_plug_the_leak

	prerequisite = {
		focus = GNG_plug_the_leak
	}

	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = GNG_our_loyalest_guardians
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GNG_our_greatest_assets"
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_our_greatest_assets_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_ibuka_modern_police_2_passed
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_our_greatest_assets_passed
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					GNG_is_pearl_river_delta_state = no
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ken_spt_temp = 2.5 }
				GNG_kenpeitai_control_change = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_our_greatest_assets_not_passed
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					GNG_is_pearl_river_delta_state = no
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ken_spt_temp = 1.25 }
				GNG_kenpeitai_control_change = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

			}

				id = guangdong_fujitsuOC.37
				hours = 6
			}
			every_owned_state = {

				}
				set_temp_variable = { yak_spt_temp = 3 }
				GNG_yakuza_control_change = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {

				id = guangdong_fujitsuOC.38
				hours = 6
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					GNG_is_pearl_river_delta_state = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { yak_spt_temp = 0.75 }
				GNG_yakuza_control_change = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp = -3 }
			GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Change = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Temp = -3 }
			GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Change = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Temp = 2.5 }
			GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Change = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Temp = 2.5 }
			GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Change = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Pre_Riots_GFT_Strength_decrease_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Pre_Riots_CCL_Strength_decrease_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Pre_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_increase_tt

	icon = GFX_focus_generic_spying_assassination
	x = 3
	y = 4
	cost = 1

	relative_position_id = GNG_do_as_i_say

	prerequisite = {
		focus = GNG_guangdong_or_anarchy
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GNG_names_names_names"
		country_event = {
			id = guangdong_hitachiRiots.55
			hours = 6
		}
		add_political_power = 35
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp = -6 }
		GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Temp = -6 }
		GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Temp = -4 }
		GNG_Despair_Change = yes
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				GNG_is_pearl_river_delta_state = no
			}
			set_temp_variable = { govt_spt_temp = 5 }
			GNG_government_control_change = yes
			set_temp_variable = { chi_app_temp = -3 }
			GNG_chinese_app_change = yes
			set_temp_variable = { zhu_app_temp = -3 }
			GNG_zhujin_app_change = yes
		}
	}
}

	}

		focus = GNG_words_from_within
	}

	prerequisite = {
		focus = GNG_names_names_names
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus GNG_the_house_always_wins"
		custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_the_house_always_wins_tt
		add_political_power = 80
		set_temp_variable = { money_reserves_temp = 0.75 }
		econ_money_reserves_change_raw_money = yes
		country_event = {
			id = guangdong_hitachiRiots.19
			hours = 6
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					GNG = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					90 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = GNG_IJA_COUP
								option = GNG_IJA_COUP_YES
							}
						}
						country_event = {
							id = guangdong_commonRiots.9
							days = 15
						}
					}
					10 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = GNG_IJA_COUP
								option = GNG_IJA_COUP_NO
							}
						}
						country_event = {
							id = guangdong_IJARiots.6
							days = 15
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
